Path: [/workspace/app-bt7xab93905d/src/pages/ArtistAvailabilityPage.tsx]

Old String: ```
  async function saveAvailability() {
```
New String: ```
  function openBatchEdit() {
    const selected = availabilities.filter((a) => selectedIds.has(a.id));
    if (selected.length === 0) return;

    // Check same artist
    const artistsInSelection = new Set(selected.map((a) => a.artist_id));
    if (artistsInSelection.size > 1) {
      toast.error('批量编辑只能针对同一个歌手');
      return;
    }

    // Compute common values
    const allSame = (key: keyof ArtistAvailability) => {
      const vals = selected.map((s) => s[key]);
      return vals.every((v) => v === vals[0]) ? vals[0] : undefined;
    };

    const typeVal = allSame('availability_type');
    const dowVal = allSame('day_of_week');
    const dateVal = allSame('specific_date');
    const startVal = allSame('available_start');
    const endVal = allSame('available_end');
    const availVal = allSame('is_available');
    const noteVal = allSame('note');

    setBatchEditForm({
      availability_type: typeVal || '',
      day_of_week: dowVal !== undefined ? dowVal : null,
      specific_date: dateVal ? dateVal.split('T')[0] : '',
      available_start: startVal || '',
      available_end: endVal || '',
      is_available: availVal !== undefined ? availVal : null,
      note: noteVal || '',
    });
    setBatchEditFields(new Set());
    setBatchEditOpen(true);
  }

  async function saveBatchEdit() {
    const selected = availabilities.filter((a) => selectedIds.has(a.id));
    if (selected.length === 0) return;

    try {
      for (const a of selected) {
        const updates: Partial<ArtistAvailability> = {};
        if (batchEditFields.has('availability_type')) {
          updates.availability_type = batchEditForm.availability_type as 'fixed' | 'temporary';
          if (updates.availability_type === 'fixed') {
            updates.specific_date = null;
          }
        }
        if (batchEditFields.has('day_of_week')) updates.day_of_week = batchEditForm.day_of_week;
        if (batchEditFields.has('specific_date')) {
          updates.specific_date = batchEditForm.specific_date || null;
          if (batchEditForm.specific_date) updates.day_of_week = null;
        }
        if (batchEditFields.has('available_start')) updates.available_start = batchEditForm.available_start || null;
        if (batchEditFields.has('available_end')) updates.available_end = batchEditForm.available_end || null;
        if (batchEditFields.has('is_available')) updates.is_available = batchEditForm.is_available!;
        if (batchEditFields.has('note')) updates.note = batchEditForm.note || null;
        if (Object.keys(updates).length > 0) {
          await updateAvailability(a.id, updates);
        }
      }
      toast.success(`已更新 ${selected.length} 条档期`);
      setBatchEditOpen(false);
      setSelectedIds(new Set());
      loadData();
    } catch (e: any) {
      toast.error('批量更新失败：' + e.message);
    }
  }
```

   438   async function saveAvailability() {
   439     if (!dialogArtistId) {
   440       toast.error('请选择歌手');
   441       return;
   442     }
   443     const payload: Partial<ArtistAvailability> = {
   444       ...availForm,
   445       artist_id: dialogArtistId,
   446     };
   447     if (availForm.availability_type === 'fixed') {
   448       payload.specific_date = null;
   449     } else {
   450       // temporary: 如果填了具体日期就用日期，否则用星期
   451       if (availForm.specific_date) {
   452         payload.day_of_week = null;
   453         payload.specific_date = availForm.specific_date.split('T')[0];
   454       } else {
   455         payload.specific_date = null;
   456       }
   457     }
   458     try {
   459       if (editingAvailId) {
   460         await updateAvailability(editingAvailId, payload);
   461         toast.success('更新成功');
   462       } else {
   463         await createAvailability(payload as any);
   464         toast.success('保存成功');
   465       }
   466       setDialogOpen(false);
   467       setEditingAvailId(null);
   468       loadData();
   469     } catch (e: any) {
   470       toast.error('保存失败：' + e.message);
   471     }
   472   }

```
  async function saveBatchEdit() {
    const selected = availabilities.filter((a) => selectedIds.has(a.id));

        const updates: Partial<ArtistAvailability> = {};

```
New String: ```
  async function saveBatchEdit() {
    const selected = availabilities.filter((a) => selectedIds.has(a.id));
    if (selected.length === 0) return;

    const first = selected[0];
    const artistId = first.artist_id;
    const existingDays = new Set<number>();
    selected.forEach((s) => {
      if (s.day_of_week !== null && s.day_of_week !== undefined) existingDays.add(s.day_of_week);
    });

    try {
      // 1. 删除取消勾选的星期
      for (const day of existingDays) {
        if (!batchEditWeekDays.has(day)) {
          const toDelete = selected.find((s) => s.day_of_week === day);
          if (toDelete) await deleteAvailability(toDelete.id);
        }
      }

      // 2. 更新保留的档期（如果勾选了其他字段）
      for (const day of batchEditWeekDays) {
        const record = selected.find((s) => s.day_of_week === day);
        if (record && batchEditFields.size > 0) {
          const updates: Partial<ArtistAvailability> = {};
          if (batchEditFields.has('availability_type')) {
            updates.availability_type = batchEditForm.availability_type as 'fixed' | 'temporary';
            if (updates.availability_type === 'fixed') updates.specific_date = null;
          }
          if (batchEditFields.has('available_start')) updates.available_start = batchEditForm.available_start || null;
          if (batchEditFields.has('available_end')) updates.available_end = batchEditForm.available_end || null;
          if (batchEditFields.has('is_available')) updates.is_available = batchEditForm.is_available!;
          if (batchEditFields.has('note')) updates.note = batchEditForm.note || null;
          if (Object.keys(updates).length > 0) {
            await updateAvailability(record.id, updates);
          }
        }
      }

      // 3. 创建新勾选的星期
      for (const day of batchEditWeekDays) {
        if (!existingDays.has(day)) {
          const payload: Partial<ArtistAvailability> = {
            artist_id: artistId,
            availability_type: (batchEditForm.availability_type as 'fixed' | 'temporary') || first.availability_type,
            day_of_week: day,
            specific_date: null,
            available_start: batchEditFields.has('available_start') ? (batchEditForm.available_start || null) : (first.available_start || '20:00'),
            available_end: batchEditFields.has('available_end') ? (batchEditForm.available_end || null) : (first.available_end || '23:00'),
            is_available: batchEditFields.has('is_available') ? batchEditForm.is_available! : first.is_available,
            note: batchEditFields.has('note') ? (batchEditForm.note || null) : first.note,
          };
          await createAvailability(payload as any);
        }
      }

      toast.success('批量更新完成');
      setBatchEditOpen(false);
      setSelectedIds(new Set());
      loadData();
    } catch (e: any) {
      toast.error('批量更新失败：' + e.message);
    }
  }
```

   571       setPasteDialogOpen(false);
   572       setPasteText('');
   573       setPastePreview([]);
   574       loadData();
   575     } catch (e: any) {
   576       toast.error('导入失败：' + e.message);
   577     }
   578   }
   579 
   580   function getArtistName(id: string) {
   581     return artists.find((a) => a.id === id)?.name || '-';
   582   }

   585

   348   async function toggleAvailabilityType(id: string, newType: 'fixed' | 'temporary') {

   358   function openBatchEdit(artistId?: string) {
   359     const selected = artistId
   360       ? availabilities.filter((a) => a.artist_id === artistId)
   361       : availabilities.filter((a) => selectedIds.has(a.id));
   362     if (selected.length === 0) return;
   363 
   364     // Check same artist
   365     const artistsInSelection = new Set(selected.map((a) => a.artist_id));
   366     if (artistsInSelection.size > 1) {
   367       toast.error('批量编辑只能针对同一个歌手');
   368       return;
   369     }
   370 
   371     // Compute common values
   372     const allSameStr = (key: 'availability_type') => {
   373       const vals = selected.map((s) => s[key]);
   374       return vals.every((v) => v === vals[0]) ? vals[0] : undefined;
   375     };
   376     const allSameNum = (key: 'day_of_week') => {
   377       const vals = selected.map((s) => s[key]);
   378       return vals.every((v) => v === vals[0]) ? vals[0] : undefined;
   379     };
   380     const allSameBool = (key: 'is_available') => {
   381       const vals = selected.map((s) => s[key]);

```
  function openBatchEdit(artistId?: string) {
    const selected = artistId
      ? availabilities.filter((a) => a.artist_id === artistId)
      : availabilities.filter((a) => selectedIds.has(a.id));
    if (selected.length === 0) return;

    // Check same artist
```

     3 const ALL_STYLES = ['R&B', '流行', '英文', '唱跳', '气氛', '抒情', '说唱'];

     6 function timeToMinutes(t: string): number {
     7   const [h, m] = t.split(':').map(Number);
     8   return h * 60 + m;
     9 }
    10 
    11 /**
    12  * 判断歌手档期是否能覆盖节次
    13  * 逻辑：节的开始时间必须在歌手可排范围内（歌手到场后 + 离场前30分钟缓冲）
    14  * 例如歌手21:30-23:00 → 有效到23:30，第3节23:30开始也能排
    15  */
    16 function canCoverSession(
    17   availStart: string,
    18   availEnd: string,
    19   sessionStart: string,
    20   _sessionEnd: string
    21 ): boolean {
    22   // 歌手来得比节开始还晚 → 不能排
    23   if (availStart > sessionStart) return false;
    24 
    25   // 给歌手结束时间加30分钟缓冲（离场/过渡时间）
    26   const availEndMin = timeToMinutes(availEnd) + 30;
    27   const sessionStartMin = timeToMinutes(sessionStart);
    28 
    29   return availEndMin >= sessionStartMin;
    30 }
    31 
    32 export function isArtistAvailable(
    33   artist: Artist,
    34   availabilities: ArtistAvailability[],
    35   date: Date,
    36   session: BarSession
    37 ): boolean {
    38   const dateStr = date.toISOString().split('T')[0];
    39   const dayOfWeek = date.getDay();
    40 
    41   // 1. Check temporary with specific_date (exact date override, highest priority)
    42   const tempExact = availabilities.find(
    43     (a) =>
    44       a.artist_id === artist.id &&
    45       a.availability_type === 'temporary' &&
    46       a.specific_date === dateStr
    47   );
    48   if (tempExact) {
    49     if (!tempExact.is_available) return false;
    50     if (
    51       !tempExact.available_start ||
    52       !tempExact.available_end ||
    53       !session.start_time ||
    54       !session.end_time
    55     ) {
    56       return true;
    57     }
    58     return canCoverSession(
    59       tempExact.available_start,
    60       tempExact.available_end,
    61       session.start_time,
    62       session.end_time
    63     );
    64   }
    65 
    66   // 2. Check temporary with day_of_week (weekly temporary schedule)
    67   const tempWeekly = availabilities.find(
    68     (a) =>
    69       a.artist_id === artist.id &&
    70       a.availability_type === 'temporary' &&
    71       a.specific_date === null &&
    72       a.day_of_week === dayOfWeek
    73   );
    74   if (tempWeekly) {
    75     if (!tempWeekly.is_available) return false;
    76     if (
    77       !tempWeekly.available_start ||
    78       !tempWeekly.available_end ||
    79       !session.start_time ||
    80       !session.end_time
    81     ) {
    82       return true;
    83     }
    84     return canCoverSession(
    85       tempWeekly.available_start,
    86       tempWeekly.available_end,
    87       session.start_time,
    88       session.end_time
    89     );
    90   }
    91 
    92   // 3. Check fixed schedule
    93   const fixedAvail = availabilities.find(
    94     (a) =>
    95       a.artist_id === artist.id &&
    96       a.availability_type === 'fixed' &&
    97       a.day_of_week === dayOfWeek
    98   );
    99 
   100   if (!fixedAvail) return false;

   124 export function hasFixedAvailability(
   125   artistId: string,
   126   availabilities: ArtistAvailability[],
   127   dayOfWeek: number
   128 ): boolean {
   129   return availabilities.some(
   130     (a) =>
   131       a.artist_id === artistId &&
   132       a.availability_type === 'fixed' &&
   133       a.day_of_week === dayOfWeek &&
   134       a.is_available
   135   );
   136 }
   137 
   138 /**
   139  * Filter available artists by style priority (degradation)
   140  * style_tags array order = priority order
   141  * e.g. [抒情, R&B, 说唱] → first try 抒情-only, then R&B-only, then 说唱-only
   142  * Returns: matched in priority order, unmatched (available but no style match), priorityGroups
   143  */
   144 export function filterAndSortArtists(
   145   artists: Artist[],
   146   availabilities: ArtistAvailability[],
   147   date: Date,
   148   session: BarSession,
   149   requiredStyles: string[]
   150 ): { matched: Artist[]; unmatched: Artist[]; priorityGroups: Artist[][] } {
   151   const allAvailable = artists.filter((a) =>
   152     isArtistAvailable(a, availabilities, date, session)
   153   );
   154 
   155   if (requiredStyles.length === 0) {
   156     return {
   157       matched: allAvailable,
   158       unmatched: [],
   159       priorityGroups: [allAvailable],
   160     };
   161   }
   162 
   163   const pickedIds = new Set<string>();
   164   const priorityGroups: Artist[][] = [];
   165   const allMatched: Artist[] = [];
   166 
   167   for (const style of requiredStyles) {
   168     const matches = allAvailable.filter(
   169       (a) => !pickedIds.has(a.id) && a.style_tags.includes(style)
   170     );
   171     priorityGroups.push(matches);
   172     for (const a of matches) {
   173       allMatched.push(a);
   174       pickedIds.add(a.id);
   175     }
   176   }
   177 
   178   const unmatched = allAvailable.filter((a) => !pickedIds.has(a.id));
   179 
   180   return { matched: allMatched, unmatched, priorityGroups };
   181 }
   182 
   183 // For auto-assign: return style-matched available artists in priority order
   184 export function filterStyleMatchedArtists(
   185   artists: Artist[],
   186   availabilities: ArtistAvailability[],
   187   date: Date,
   188   session: BarSession,
   189   requiredStyles: string[]
   190 ): Artist[] {
   191   const { matched } = filterAndSortArtists(
   192     artists,
   193     availabilities,
   194     date,
   195     session,
   196     requiredStyles
   197   );
   198   return matched;
   199 }

    98 export async function getBarSessions(barId: string, weekday?: number): Promise<BarSession[]> {
    99   let q = supabase.from('bar_sessions').select('*').eq('bar_id', barId).order('session_number');
   100   if (weekday !== undefined) {
   101     q = q.eq('weekday', weekday);
   102   } else {
   103     // Return both weekday-specific and null (generic) when no weekday filter
   104     // Actually for the full list view we want all, but for schedule generation we want a specific weekday
   105   }
   106   const { data, error } = await q;
   107   if (error) throw error;
   108   return Array.isArray(data) ? data : [];
   109 }

   111 export async function getBarSessionsForDate(barId: string, weekday: number): Promise<BarSession[]> {
   112   // First try weekday-specific config
   113   const { data: specific, error: err1 } = await supabase
   114     .from('bar_sessions')
   115     .select('*')
   116     .eq('bar_id', barId)
   117     .eq('weekday', weekday)
   118     .order('session_number');
   119   if (err1) throw err1;
   120   if (specific && specific.length > 0) return specific;
   121   // Fallback to generic config (weekday is null)
   122   const { data: generic, error: err2 } = await supabase
   123     .from('bar_sessions')
   124     .select('*')
   125     .eq('bar_id', barId)
   126     .is('weekday', null)
   127     .order('session_number');
   128   if (err2) throw err2;
   129   return Array.isArray(generic) ? generic : [];

AgentThinkAction(thought='找到核心bug了！\n\n`canCoverSession` 函数在处理跨天节次（如第4节 01:00-01:30）时有严重bug：\n\n- sessionStart = "01:00" → 60分钟\n- availEnd = "23:00" → 1380分钟\n- availEndMin = 1380 + 30 = 1410\n- 1410 >= 60 → true ❌\n\n但实际上23:00是当天晚上，01:00是次日凌晨。歌手23:00离场后不可能参加凌晨01:00的节次！\n\n这是因为 `timeToMinutes` 把01:00当作了当天的60分钟（实际上应该是次日凌晨），而23:00是1380分钟，所以23:00 > 01:00。\n\n修复方案：当 sessionStart < "06:00"（跨天凌晨节次）且 availEnd >= "12:00"（当天晚上离场），则不能覆盖。\n\n另外用户的第2个需求"所有档期匹配的歌手都要放进可选歌手里"——现在弹窗已经显示了 matched 和 unmatched 歌手，但可能因为时间匹配bug，某些歌手被错误地排除在 allAvailable 之外。修复时间匹配bug后，这些歌手就会正确出现了。', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

Old String: ```
/**
 * 判断歌手档期是否能覆盖节次
 * 逻辑：节的开始时间必须在歌手可排范围内（歌手到场后 + 离场前30分钟缓冲）
 * 例如歌手21:30-23:00 → 有效到23:30，第3节23:30开始也能排
 */
function canCoverSession(
  availStart: string,
  availEnd: string,
  sessionStart: string,
  _sessionEnd: string
): boolean {
  // 歌手来得比节开始还晚 → 不能排
  if (availStart > sessionStart) return false;

  // 给歌手结束时间加30分钟缓冲（离场/过渡时间）
  const availEndMin = timeToMinutes(availEnd) + 30;
  const sessionStartMin = timeToMinutes(sessionStart);

  return availEndMin >= sessionStartMin;
}
```
New String: ```
/**
 * 判断歌手档期是否能覆盖节次
 * 逻辑：节的开始时间必须在歌手可排范围内（歌手到场后 + 离场前30分钟缓冲）
 * 例如歌手21:30-23:00 → 有效到23:30，第3节23:30开始也能排
 * 
 * 跨天处理：节次在凌晨（如01:00）属于第二天，歌手当天晚上（如23:00）离场不能覆盖
 */
function canCoverSession(
  availStart: string,
  availEnd: string,
  sessionStart: string,
  _sessionEnd: string
): boolean {
  // 歌手来得比节开始还晚 → 不能排
  if (availStart > sessionStart) return false;

  // 跨天节次检查：session 在凌晨（如01:00），但歌手是当天晚上（如23:00）
  // 这种情况下歌手已离场，不能覆盖次日凌晨节次
  if (sessionStart < '06:00' && availEnd >= '12:00') {
    return false;
  }

  // 给歌手结束时间加30分钟缓冲（离场/过渡时间）
  const availEndMin = timeToMinutes(availEnd) + 30;
  const sessionStartMin = timeToMinutes(sessionStart);

  return availEndMin >= sessionStartMin;
}
```

```
/**
 * 判断歌手档期是否能覆盖节次
 * 逻辑：节的开始时间必须在歌手可排范围内（歌手到场后 + 离场前30分钟缓冲）
 * 例如歌手21:30-23:00 → 有效到23:30，第3节23:30开始也能排
 * 
 * 跨天处理：当 sessionStart 在凌晨（<06:00）且歌手当天晚上离场（>=12:00），视为已离场不能覆盖
 */
function canCoverSession(
  availStart: string,
  availEnd: string,
  sessionStart: string,
  _sessionEnd: string
): boolean {
  // 歌手来得比节次开始还晚 → 不能排
  if (availStart > sessionStart) return false;

  // 跨天节次检查：session 在凌晨（如01:00），但歌手是当天晚上（如23:00）
  // 这种情况下歌手已离场，不能覆盖次日凌晨节次
  if (sessionStart < '06:00' && availEnd >= '12:00') {
    return false;
  }

  // 给歌手结束时间加30分钟缓冲（离场/过渡时间）
  const availEndMin = timeToMinutes(availEnd) + 30;
  const sessionStartMin = timeToMinutes(sessionStart);

  return availEndMin >= sessionStartMin;
}
```
New String: ```
/**
 * 判断歌手档期是否能覆盖节次
 * 逻辑：
 * - 正常节次：歌手必须来得不晚于节次开始，且离场不早于节次结束（+30分钟缓冲）
 * - 跨天节次（次日凌晨）：歌手当天晚上在场即可放宽匹配
 */
function canCoverSession(
  availStart: string,
  availEnd: string,
  sessionStart: string,
  sessionEnd: string
): boolean {
  // 跨天节次（次日凌晨如01:00）：放宽匹配
  if (sessionStart < '06:00') {
    // 歌手当天晚上在场（开始 >= 18:00 且离场 >= 20:00），允许排
    if (availStart >= '18:00' && availEnd >= '20:00') return true;
    // 歌手跨天工作到次日凌晨
    if (availEnd < '06:00') {
      const availEndMin = timeToMinutes(availEnd);
      const sessionEndMin = timeToMinutes(sessionEnd);
      return availEndMin + 30 >= sessionEndMin;
    }
    return false;
  }

  // 正常节次：歌手来得不比节次晚
  if (availStart > sessionStart) return false;

  // 歌手必须覆盖到节次结束（+30分钟缓冲）
  const availEndMin = timeToMinutes(availEnd);
  const sessionEndMin = timeToMinutes(sessionEnd);
  return availEndMin + 30 >= sessionEndMin;
}
```

    45 export function isArtistAvailable(
    46   artist: Artist,
    47   availabilities: ArtistAvailability[],
    48   date: Date,
    49   session: BarSession
    50 ): boolean {
    51   const dateStr = date.toISOString().split('T')[0];
    52   const dayOfWeek = date.getDay();
    53 
    54   // 1. Check temporary with specific_date (exact date override, highest priority)
    55   const tempExact = availabilities.find(
    56     (a) =>
    57       a.artist_id === artist.id &&
    58       a.availability_type === 'temporary' &&
    59       a.specific_date === dateStr
    60   );
    61   if (tempExact) {
    62     if (!tempExact.is_available) return false;
    63     if (
    64       !tempExact.available_start ||
    65       !tempExact.available_end ||
    66       !session.start_time ||
    67       !session.end_time
    68     ) {
    69       return true;
    70     }
    71     return canCoverSession(
    72       tempExact.available_start,
    73       tempExact.available_end,
    74       session.start_time,
    75       session.end_time
    76     );
    77   }
    78 
    79   // 2. Check temporary with day_of_week (weekly temporary schedule)
    80   const tempWeekly = availabilities.find(
    81     (a) =>
    82       a.artist_id === artist.id &&
    83       a.availability_type === 'temporary' &&
    84       a.specific_date === null &&
    85       a.day_of_week === dayOfWeek
    86   );
    87   if (tempWeekly) {
    88     if (!tempWeekly.is_available) return false;
    89     if (
    90       !tempWeekly.available_start ||
    91       !tempWeekly.available_end ||
    92       !session.start_time ||
    93       !session.end_time
    94     ) {
    95       return true;

   100       session.start_time,
   101       session.end_time
   102     );

   107     (a) =>
   108       a.artist_id === artist.id &&
   109       a.availability_type === 'fixed' &&
   110       a.day_of_week === dayOfWeek

   356 export async function getSchedules(barId?: string): Promise<Schedule[]> {
   357   let q = supabase.from('schedules').select('*').order('created_at', { ascending: false });
   358   if (barId) q = q.eq('bar_id', barId);

   361   return Array.isArray(data) ? data : [];
   362 }

New String: ```
  async function loadSchedules() {
    const sc = await getSchedules();
    setSchedules(sc);
    setSelectedIds(new Set());
  }

  function toggleSelect(id: string) {
    setSelectedIds((prev) => {
      const next = new Set(prev);
      if (next.has(id)) next.delete(id);
      else next.add(id);
      return next;
    });
  }

  const isAllSelected = filtered.length > 0 && filtered.every((s) => selectedIds.has(s.id));

  function toggleSelectAll() {
    if (isAllSelected) {
      setSelectedIds((prev) => {
        const next = new Set(prev);
        filtered.forEach((s) => next.delete(s.id));
        return next;
      });
    } else {
      setSelectedIds((prev) => {
        const next = new Set(prev);
        filtered.forEach((s) => next.add(s.id));
        return next;
      });
    }
  }

  async function handleDeleteSingle(id: string) {
    try {
      await deleteSchedule(id);
      toast.success('删除成功');
      setSelectedIds((prev) => {
        const next = new Set(prev);
        next.delete(id);
        return next;
      });
      loadSchedules();
    } catch (e: any) {
      toast.error('删除失败：' + e.message);
    }
  }

  async function handleDeleteBatch() {
    if (selectedIds.size === 0) return;
    try {
      await deleteSchedules(Array.from(selectedIds));
      toast.success(`成功删除 ${selectedIds.size} 条排班`);
      setSelectedIds(new Set());
      loadSchedules();
    } catch (e: any) {
      toast.error('批量删除失败：' + e.message);
    }
  }
```

     6 function timeToMinutes(t: string): number {
     7   const [h, m] = t.split(':').map(Number);
     8   return h * 60 + m;
     9 }
    10 
    11 /**
    12  * 判断歌手档期是否能覆盖节次
    13  * 逻辑：
    14  * - 正常节次：歌手必须来得不晚于节次开始，且离场不早于节次结束（+30分钟缓冲）
    15  * - 跨天节次（次日凌晨）：歌手当天晚上在场即可放宽匹配
    16  */
    17 function canCoverSession(
    18   availStart: string,
    19   availEnd: string,
    20   sessionStart: string,
    21   sessionEnd: string
    22 ): boolean {
    23   // 跨天节次（次日凌晨如01:00）：放宽匹配
    24   if (sessionStart < '06:00') {
    25     // 歌手当天晚上在场（开始 >= 18:00 且离场 >= 20:00），允许排
    26     if (availStart >= '18:00' && availEnd >= '20:00') return true;
    27     // 歌手跨天工作到次日凌晨
    28     if (availEnd < '06:00') {
    29       const availEndMin = timeToMinutes(availEnd);
    30       const sessionEndMin = timeToMinutes(sessionEnd);
    31       return availEndMin + 30 >= sessionEndMin;
    32     }
    33     return false;
    34   }
    35 
    36   // 正常节次：歌手来得不比节次晚
    37   if (availStart > sessionStart) return false;
    38 
    39   // 歌手必须覆盖到节次结束（+30分钟缓冲）
    40   const availEndMin = timeToMinutes(availEnd);
    41   const sessionEndMin = timeToMinutes(sessionEnd);
    42   return availEndMin + 30 >= sessionEndMin;
    43 }

    45 export function isArtistAvailable(
    46   artist: Artist,
    47   availabilities: ArtistAvailability[],
    48   date: Date,
    49   session: BarSession
    50 ): boolean {
    51   const dateStr = date.toISOString().split('T')[0];
    52   const dayOfWeek = date.getDay();
    53 
    54   // 1. Check temporary with specific_date (exact date override, highest priority)
    55   const tempExact = availabilities.find(
    56     (a) =>
    57       a.artist_id === artist.id &&
    58       a.availability_type === 'temporary' &&
    59       a.specific_date === dateStr
    60   );
    61   if (tempExact) {
    62     if (!tempExact.is_available) return false;
    63     if (
    64       !tempExact.available_start ||
    65       !tempExact.available_end ||
    66       !session.start_time ||
    67       !session.end_time
    68     ) {
    69       return true;
    70     }
    71     return canCoverSession(
    72       tempExact.available_start,
    73       tempExact.available_end,
    74       session.start_time,
    75       session.end_time
    76     );
    77   }
    78 
    79   // 2. Check temporary with day_of_week (weekly temporary schedule)
    80   const tempWeekly = availabilities.find(
    81     (a) =>
    82       a.artist_id === artist.id &&
    83       a.availability_type === 'temporary' &&
    84       a.specific_date === null &&
    85       a.day_of_week === dayOfWeek
    86   );
    87   if (tempWeekly) {
    88     if (!tempWeekly.is_available) return false;
    89     if (
    90       !tempWeekly.available_start ||
    91       !tempWeekly.available_end ||
    92       !session.start_time ||
    93       !session.end_time
    94     ) {
    95       return true;
    96     }
    97     return canCoverSession(
    98       tempWeekly.available_start,
    99       tempWeekly.available_end,
   100       session.start_time,
   101       session.end_time
   102     );
   103   }
   104 
   105   // 3. Check fixed schedule
   106   const fixedAvail = availabilities.find(
   107     (a) =>
   108       a.artist_id === artist.id &&
   109       a.availability_type === 'fixed' &&
   110       a.day_of_week === dayOfWeek
   111   );
   112 
   113   if (!fixedAvail) return false;
   114   if (!fixedAvail.is_available) return false;
   115 
   116   if (
   117     !fixedAvail.available_start ||
   118     !fixedAvail.available_end ||
   119     !session.start_time ||
   120     !session.end_time
   121   ) {
   122     return true;
   123   }
   124 
   125   return canCoverSession(
   126     fixedAvail.available_start,
   127     fixedAvail.available_end,
   128     session.start_time,
   129     session.end_time
   130   );
   131 }
   132 
   133 /**
   134  * Check if artist has fixed availability (not temporary override)
   135  * Used to identify fixed-slot singers for auto-locking
   136  */
   137 export function hasFixedAvailability(
   138   artistId: string,
   139   availabilities: ArtistAvailability[],
   140   dayOfWeek: number
   141 ): boolean {
   142   return availabilities.some(
   143     (a) =>
   144       a.artist_id === artistId &&
   145       a.availability_type === 'fixed' &&
   146       a.day_of_week === dayOfWeek &&
   147       a.is_available
   148   );
   149 }
   150 
   151 /**
   152  * Filter available artists by style priority (degradation)
   153  * style_tags array order = priority order
   154  * e.g. [抒情, R&B, 说唱] → first try 抒情-only, then R&B-only, then 说唱-only
   155  * Returns: matched in priority order, unmatched (available but no style match), priorityGroups
   156  */
   157 export function filterAndSortArtists(
   158   artists: Artist[],
   159   availabilities: ArtistAvailability[],
   160   date: Date,
   161   session: BarSession,
   162   requiredStyles: string[]
   163 ): { matched: Artist[]; unmatched: Artist[]; priorityGroups: Artist[][] } {
   164   const allAvailable = artists.filter((a) =>
   165     isArtistAvailable(a, availabilities, date, session)
   166   );
   167 
   168   if (requiredStyles.length === 0) {
   169     return {
   170       matched: allAvailable,
   171       unmatched: [],
   172       priorityGroups: [allAvailable],
   173     };
   174   }
   175 
   176   const pickedIds = new Set<string>();
   177   const priorityGroups: Artist[][] = [];
   178   const allMatched: Artist[] = [];
   179 
   180   for (const style of requiredStyles) {
   181     const matches = allAvailable.filter(
   182       (a) => !pickedIds.has(a.id) && a.style_tags.includes(style)
   183     );
   184     priorityGroups.push(matches);
   185     for (const a of matches) {
   186       allMatched.push(a);
   187       pickedIds.add(a.id);
   188     }
   189   }
   190 
   191   const unmatched = allAvailable.filter((a) => !pickedIds.has(a.id));
   192 
   193   return { matched: allMatched, unmatched, priorityGroups };
   194 }
   195 
   196 // For auto-assign: return style-matched available artists in priority order
   197 export function filterStyleMatchedArtists(
   198   artists: Artist[],
   199   availabilities: ArtistAvailability[],
   200   date: Date,
   201   session: BarSession,
   202   requiredStyles: string[]
   203 ): Artist[] {
   204   const { matched } = filterAndSortArtists(
   205     artists,
   206     availabilities,
   207     date,
   208     session,
   209     requiredStyles
   210   );
   211   return matched;
   212 }

   214 export function getPeriodLabel(type: 'weekly' | 'monthly', date: Date): string {
   215   const y = date.getFullYear();
   216   if (type === 'monthly') {
   217     const m = date.getMonth() + 1;
   218     return `${y}年${m}月`;
   219   }
   220   const startOfYear = new Date(y, 0, 1);
   221   const day = startOfYear.getDay();
   222   const offset = day === 0 ? 0 : 7 - day;
   223   const firstMonday = new Date(y, 0, 1 + offset);
   224   const diff = date.getTime() - firstMonday.getTime();
   225   const weekNum = Math.floor(diff / (7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000)) + 1;
   226   return `${y}年第${weekNum}周`;
   227 }
   228 
   229 export function getPeriodStart(type: 'weekly' | 'monthly', date: Date): Date {
   230   if (type === 'monthly') {
   231     return new Date(date.getFullYear(), date.getMonth(), 1);
   232   }
   233   const d = new Date(date);
   234   const day = d.getDay();
   235   const diff = d.getDate() - day + (day === 0 ? -6 : 1);
   236   return new Date(d.setDate(diff));
   237 }
   238 
   239 export function getPeriodEnd(type: 'weekly' | 'monthly', date: Date): Date {
   240   if (type === 'monthly') {
   241     return new Date(date.getFullYear(), date.getMonth() + 1, 0);
   242   }
   243   const start = getPeriodStart(type, date);
   244   const end = new Date(start);
   245   end.setDate(start.getDate() + 6);
   246   return end;
   247 }
   248 
   249 export function getDatesInPeriod(start: Date, end: Date): Date[] {
   250   const dates: Date[] = [];
   251   const curr = new Date(start);
   252   while (curr <= end) {
   253     dates.push(new Date(curr));
   254     curr.setDate(curr.getDate() + 1);
   255   }
   256   return dates;
   257 }
   258 
   259 export function autoAssign(
   260   artists: Artist[],
   261   availabilities: ArtistAvailability[],
   262   sessions: BarSession[],
   263   dates: Date[],
   264   restDays: number[] = []
   265 ): Record<string, string[]> {
   266   const result: Record<string, string[]> = {};
   267   const showCount: Record<string, number> = {};
   268   artists.forEach((a) => (showCount[a.id] = 0));
   269 
   270   for (const date of dates) {
   271     const dayOfWeek = date.getDay();
   272     // Skip rest days
   273     if (restDays.includes(dayOfWeek)) continue;
   274 
   275     for (const session of sessions) {
   276       const dateStr = date.toISOString().split('T')[0];
   277       const key = `${dateStr}_${session.id}`;
   278       const needed = session.singers_per_session;
   279 
   280       // Step 1: Auto-lock fixed-slot singers
   281       const locked: string[] = [];
   282       for (const artist of artists) {
   283         if (locked.length >= needed) break;
   284         if (
   285           hasFixedAvailability(artist.id, availabilities, dayOfWeek) &&
   286           isArtistAvailable(artist, availabilities, date, session)
   287         ) {
   288           locked.push(artist.id);
   289           showCount[artist.id] = (showCount[artist.id] || 0) + 1;
   290         }
   291       }
   292 
   293       // Step 2: Fill remaining slots with style-matched available artists
   294       const remainingNeeded = needed - locked.length;
   295       const styleMatched = filterStyleMatchedArtists(
   296         artists.filter((a) => !locked.includes(a.id)),
   297         availabilities,
   298         date,
   299         session,
   300         session.style_tags || []
   301       );
   302 
   303       // Sort by show count for balanced distribution
   304       const sorted = [...styleMatched].sort(
   305         (a, b) => (showCount[a.id] || 0) - (showCount[b.id] || 0)
   306       );
   307 
   308       const picked: string[] = [];
   309       for (const artist of sorted) {
   310         if (picked.length >= remainingNeeded) break;
   311         picked.push(artist.id);
   312         showCount[artist.id] = (showCount[artist.id] || 0) + 1;
   313       }
   314 
   315       result[key] = [...locked, ...picked];
   316     }
   317   }
   318 
   319   return result;
   320 }

Old String: ```
/**
 * 判断歌手档期是否能覆盖节次
 * 逻辑：
 * - 正常节次：歌手必须来得不晚于节次开始，且离场不早于节次结束（+30分钟缓冲）
 * - 跨天节次（次日凌晨）：歌手当天晚上在场即可放宽匹配
 */
function canCoverSession(
  availStart: string,
  availEnd: string,
  sessionStart: string,
  sessionEnd: string
): boolean {
  // 跨天节次（次日凌晨如01:00）：放宽匹配
  if (sessionStart < '06:00') {
    // 歌手当天晚上在场（开始 >= 18:00 且离场 >= 20:00），允许排
    if (availStart >= '18:00' && availEnd >= '20:00') return true;
    // 歌手跨天工作到次日凌晨
    if (availEnd < '06:00') {
      const availEndMin = timeToMinutes(availEnd);
      const sessionEndMin = timeToMinutes(sessionEnd);
      return availEndMin + 30 >= sessionEndMin;
    }
    return false;
  }

  // 正常节次：歌手来得不比节次晚
  if (availStart > sessionStart) return false;

  // 歌手必须覆盖到节次结束（+30分钟缓冲）
  const availEndMin = timeToMinutes(availEnd);
  const sessionEndMin = timeToMinutes(sessionEnd);
  return availEndMin + 30 >= sessionEndMin;
}
```
New String: ```
/**
 * 判断歌手档期是否能覆盖节次
 * 逻辑：
 * - 凌晨节次（<06:00，如01:00）：歌手当天晚上在场即可，不检查精确时间重叠
 * - 正常节次：歌手来得不晚于节次开始，且离场不早于节次结束（+30分钟缓冲）
 */
function canCoverSession(
  availStart: string,
  availEnd: string,
  sessionStart: string,
  sessionEnd: string
): boolean {
  // 凌晨节次（< 06:00）：歌手当天晚上在场即可
  if (sessionStart < '06:00') {
    return availStart < '23:59' && availEnd >= '18:00';
  }

  // 正常节次：歌手来得不比节次晚
  if (availStart > sessionStart) return false;

  // 歌手必须覆盖到节次结束（+30分钟缓冲）
  const availEndMin = timeToMinutes(availEnd);
  const sessionEndMin = timeToMinutes(sessionEnd);
  return availEndMin + 30 >= sessionEndMin;
}
```

```
      // Step 1: Auto-lock fixed-slot singers, style-matched first
      const styleTags = session.style_tags || [];
      const fixedCandidates = artists.filter(
        (a) =>
          hasFixedAvailability(a.id, availabilities, dayOfWeek) &&
          isArtistAvailable(a, availabilities, date, session)
      );
      // Sort: style-matched first, then by show count (balanced)
      const sortedFixed = [...fixedCandidates].sort((a, b) => {
        const aStyleMatch = styleTags.some((st) => a.style_tags.includes(st)) ? 1 : 0;
        const bStyleMatch = styleTags.some((st) => b.style_tags.includes(st)) ? 1 : 0;
        if (bStyleMatch !== aStyleMatch) return bStyleMatch - aStyleMatch;
        return (showCount[a.id] || 0) - (showCount[b.id] || 0);
      });
      const locked: string[] = [];
      for (const artist of sortedFixed) {
        if (locked.length >= needed) break;
        locked.push(artist.id);
```

```
  const addExternal = async (name: string) => {
    if (!schedule || !name.trim()) return;
    const [date, sessionId] = cellKey.split('_');
    try {
      const trimmedName = name.trim();
      // 匹配歌手池中同名歌手，自动关联
      const matchedArtist = poolArtists.find(
        (a) => a.name === trimmedName
      );
      await upsertAssignments([{
        schedule_id: schedule.id,
        date,
        session_id: sessionId,
        artist_id: matchedArtist ? matchedArtist.id : undefined,

    } catch (e: any) {

    }
```

    11 /**
    12  * 判断歌手档期是否能覆盖节次
    13  * 逻辑：
    14  * - 凌晨节次（<06:00，如01:00）：歌手当天晚上在场即可，不检查精确时间重叠
    15  * - 正常节次：歌手来得不晚于节次开始，且离场不早于节次结束（+30分钟缓冲）
    16  */
    17 function canCoverSession(
    18   availStart: string,
    19   availEnd: string,
    20   sessionStart: string,
    21   sessionEnd: string
    22 ): boolean {
    23   // 凌晨节次（< 06:00）：歌手当天晚上在场即可
    24   if (sessionStart < '06:00') {
    25     return availStart < '23:59' && availEnd >= '18:00';
    26   }
    27 
    28   // 正常节次：歌手来得不比节次晚
    29   if (availStart > sessionStart) return false;
    30 
    31   // 歌手必须覆盖到节次结束（+30分钟缓冲）
    32   const availEndMin = timeToMinutes(availEnd);
    33   const sessionEndMin = timeToMinutes(sessionEnd);
    34   return availEndMin + 30 >= sessionEndMin;
    35 }
    36 
    37 export function isArtistAvailable(
    38   artist: Artist,
    39   availabilities: ArtistAvailability[],
    40   date: Date,
    41   session: BarSession
    42 ): boolean {
    43   const dateStr = date.toISOString().split('T')[0];
    44   const dayOfWeek = date.getDay();
    45 
    46   // 1. Check temporary with specific_date (exact date override, highest priority)
    47   const tempExact = availabilities.find(
    48     (a) =>
    49       a.artist_id === artist.id &&
    50       a.availability_type === 'temporary' &&
    51       a.specific_date === dateStr
    52   );
    53   if (tempExact && tempExact.is_available) {
    54     if (
    55       !tempExact.available_start ||
    56       !tempExact.available_end ||
    57       !session.start_time ||
    58       !session.end_time
    59     ) {
    60       return true;
    61     }
    62     return canCoverSession(
    63       tempExact.available_start,
    64       tempExact.available_end,
    65       session.start_time,
    66       session.end_time
    67     );
    68   }
    69   // tempExact 存在但 is_available=false → 继续查 fixed（不直接阻断）
    70 
    71   // 2. Check temporary with day_of_week (weekly temporary schedule)
    72   const tempWeekly = availabilities.find(
    73     (a) =>
    74       a.artist_id === artist.id &&
    75       a.availability_type === 'temporary' &&
    76       a.specific_date === null &&
    77       a.day_of_week === dayOfWeek
    78   );
    79   if (tempWeekly && tempWeekly.is_available) {
    80     if (
    81       !tempWeekly.available_start ||
    82       !tempWeekly.available_end ||
    83       !session.start_time ||
    84       !session.end_time
    85     ) {

   260   artists.forEach((a) => (showCount[a.id] = 0));
   261 
   262   for (const date of dates) {
   263     const dayOfWeek = date.getDay();
   264     // Skip rest days
   265     if (restDays.includes(dayOfWeek)) continue;
   266 
   267     for (const session of sessions) {
   268       const dateStr = date.toISOString().split('T')[0];
   269       const key = `${dateStr}_${session.id}`;
   270       const needed = session.singers_per_session;
   271 
   272       // Step 1: Auto-lock fixed-slot singers, style-matched first
   273       const styleTags = session.style_tags || [];
   274       const fixedCandidates = artists.filter(
   275         (a) =>
   276           hasFixedAvailability(a.id, availabilities, dayOfWeek) &&
   277           isArtistAvailable(a, availabilities, date, session)
   278       );
   279       // Sort: style-matched first, then by show count (balanced)
   280       const sortedFixed = [...fixedCandidates].sort((a, b) => {
   281         const aStyleMatch = styleTags.some((st) => a.style_tags.includes(st)) ? 1 : 0;
   282         const bStyleMatch = styleTags.some((st) => b.style_tags.includes(st)) ? 1 : 0;
   283         if (bStyleMatch !== aStyleMatch) return bStyleMatch - aStyleMatch;
   284         return (showCount[a.id] || 0) - (showCount[b.id] || 0);
   285       });
   286       const locked: string[] = [];
   287       for (const artist of sortedFixed) {
   288         if (locked.length >= needed) break;
   289         locked.push(artist.id);
   290         showCount[artist.id] = (showCount[artist.id] || 0) + 1;
   291       }
   292 
   293       // Step 2: Fill remaining slots with style-matched available artists
   294       const remainingNeeded = needed - locked.length;
   295       const styleMatched = filterStyleMatchedArtists(
   296         artists.filter((a) => !locked.includes(a.id)),
   297         availabilities,
   298         date,
   299         session,
   300         session.style_tags || []
   301       );
   302 
   303       // Sort by show count for balanced distribution
   304       const sorted = [...styleMatched].sort(
   305         (a, b) => (showCount[a.id] || 0) - (showCount[b.id] || 0)
   306       );
   307 
   308       const picked: string[] = [];
   309       for (const artist of sorted) {
   310         if (picked.length >= remainingNeeded) break;
   311         picked.push(artist.id);
   312         showCount[artist.id] = (showCount[artist.id] || 0) + 1;
   313       }
   314 
   315       result[key] = [...locked, ...picked];
   316     }
   317   }
   318 
   319   return result;
   320 }
